 Let's know 5 such tips that you can run your smartphone for a long time without charging the phone battery again and again
 1
 Reduce the brightness of the phone's screen, in a smart phone with a touch screen, it spends about half the battery screen
 screen jitani badi, chamakdaar or hai rijolution vaali hogi use power bhi utani hi zyada chahie
 The way to do this is if your phone has auto mode for screen brightness then use it, otherwise keep the brightness around 50%
 isse aapaki aakhon par jor bhi kam padegaa or betry bhi kam kharch hogi
 2
 live walpaper kaa moh chodenenemated wallpaper to sabhi ko pasand hote hai lekin vastav main ye saadhaaran walpaper kii tulana main zyada betry kharch karte hai
 Live wallpapers like floating fish, moving leaves on the phone screen look beautiful
 lekin ye betry ke bade dushman hai
 Therefore, it is advisable for you to make a wallpaper of any dark color instead of such wallpaper
 3
 Do not keep apps on auto update mode
 All the apps of Android phone keep updating
 iskaa sabase bada nuksaan yah he ki isse aapke phone kii betry or data chargeej donon hi kharch hote hai
 So always keep the auto update turned off and update the app when needed
 saath hi phaltu ke ap jo aapke kaam ke nahin hai unhen install karne se bachein
 4

 5

 Being on the app background like Facebook, Twitter, Gmail, Office Mail, Google Plus, they spend the battery on your phone

 Was Chidambaram's seal on every decision of the king? Did Chidambaram know about the 2G spectrum scam? These are the questions on which the country's largest court will decide
 supreme court ke justise ji es singhvi or justise e ke ganguli kii khandpeeth yachikakarta subramanyam swami kii arji par apana faisla sunayegi
 Swamy has demanded in his application that the CBI be ordered to investigate the role of Chidambaram in the 2G scam
 swami ke mutabik raja ke har faisle par chidambaram kii muhar thi or wo spactrum kii keemat bagaiyr chidambaram kii hari jhandi ke tay hi nahin kar sakate the
 Swamy has submitted a complete account of the correspondence between the two ministries and a long list of documents with his application
 is maamle main sibiai chidambaram ko puri tarah se clin chit de chuki he
 The CBI says that the case is already pending in the lower court and Swamy should put his side there
 centre sarkaar ne daleel di ki jab 2ji ghotaale kaa sangyaan vishesh adaalat le chuki he, kisi vyakti vishesh kii jaanch yaa phir aage kii jaanch se jude tamaam sawaal sirf or sirf nichali adaalat hi tay kar sakati he
 Therefore, the Supreme Court does not need to order Swamy's application
 2ji spectrum kii daldal main upie sarkaar ke purv sanchaar mantri raja, sarkaar ke aalaa afasar or topshot industrialist fanse hai- ab kya chidambaram kii baari he? gend supreme court ke paale main he lekin itnaa tay he ki is faisle kaa asar na sirf chidambaram ke rajnatik bhavishya par padegaa balki sarkaar ke bhavishya par bhi
 The Supreme Court is going to take another important decision for the telecom sector
 court ye faisla sunayega ki 2 ji spectrum ke 122 license radd kiye jaaenge yaa nahin
 Public interest petitioner Center of Public Interstate Litigation has demanded that the allocation of spectrum in 2008 at 2001 prices was wrong, hence the entire allocation should be canceled as it has caused a loss of crores to the government
 ye bhi maang kii gai ki bhavishya main sirf nilaamee ke jariye hi spectrum kaa aavanton kiya janaa chahie
 For the last few days, most of the incidents in the country are being tried to give communal color with the help of social media
 ek video soshal media par in dinon teji se viral ho rahaa he
 In this, some boys are seen beating a girl brutally
 video ke saath daawa kiya ja rahaa he ki ye sab muslim ladke badla lene ke liye hindu ladki ko peet rahe hai
 India Today's anti-fake News War Room (AFWA) found in the investigation that the claim made with the viral video is misleading
 yah ghatana madhya pradesh ke dhar jile kii he jahaan ek dalit ladke se prem prasang ke chalate ladki ke rishtedaaron ne uski dhunaai kar di
 The archived version of the post can be viewed
 twitororafesbukapar share ho rahe is video main dekha ja saktaa he kis tarah aath se das ladke ek ladki ko sadak kinare peet rahe hai
 The caption accompanying the video reads: 'how 8-10 boys are killing a girl together!' Such people are happening somewhere, not humans but Satan
 ’viral video ko reverse search karne par hamen madhya pradesh ke dhar jile main hui is ghatana se sambandhit ekanyuj articalamila
 According to media reports, the incident occurred on 25 June
 video main najar aa rahi ladki adivasee he or use peetane vaale log uske hi rishtedaar hai
 The girl's family members were angry with her love affair with a Dalit boy
 media reports ke anusaar kuch dinon pehle yah ladki apane premi ke saath ghar se bhaag gai thi, lekin kuch hi dinon main police ne unhen pakad liya or ladki ko uske gharavaalon ko saunp diya
 His family members wanted him to marry a boy of Bhilala caste
 jab ladki ne isse inkaar kiya to uske gharavaalon ne 25 june ko use is tarah khuleam peet diya
 ASP Rupesh Dwivedi said: 'A girl from the village of Thana tiger had gone with a boy, which had recorded her missing
 ladki balig thi
 When the girl was caught, she agreed to accompany her parents
 subah kareeb 10 baje vah ladki ghar gai
 Later in the afternoon there was a conversation between these people after which the girl's family and her brothers assaulted her
 jaisaa ki video main dikh rahaa he, wo log ladki ke saath kaaphi galat tareeke se pesh aae
 As soon as the police got information, action was taken by the police
 exiaar darj kii gai he jisamen saat logon ko namjad kiya gaya he
 Four persons have been detained, including his brother
 poochtacha kii ja rahi he
 'many reputed media institutes have published this event
 padtaal main saaf hua ki viral video prem prasang se sambandhit he, soshal media par ise galat dhang se sampradayik rang dene kii koshish kii ja rahi he
 a week ago, yoga guru Baba Ramdev and former Army Chief V
 in demonstrations against mass rape with a 23-year-old girl
 ke
 Singh also joined
 unhone ghatana ke khilaaf aawaaj uthaane vaale pradarshnakariyon par karrwai ke liye police kii ninda kii
 The yoga guru reached Jantar Mantar standing on the roof of a bus and addressed the people along with the former army chief
 yoga guru ne jab mukhya pradarshan sthal india get kii ore badhane kaa prayaas kiya to police ne unhen do kilometre pehle hi roak diya
 a colleague of the yoga guru reported that Ramdev and V
 ke
 As soon as Singh finished his address, the police surrounded the area and did not allow him to leave the place
 yoga guru ke ek sahyogi ne bataaya ki unhone jantar mantar par bairicade laga diya jisase ham aage nahin ja sake
 When some of Baba Ramdev's supporters attempted to break the barricade, he allegedly got into a scuffle with the police in which two people were injured
 jantar mantar par bairicade laga die gaye or hamen kahin jane kii ijaajat nahin di gai
 Addressing the people, Baba Ramdev blamed the police for not providing adequate security to women on the streets
 unhone kaha ki sarkaar ko twarit adaalatein gathit kerani chahie or sabhi dushkarmiyon ko sajaa deni chahie

 But in order to get a new smartphone, a big problem is what to do with your old smartphone in the face of the new one? Although many people do not think of anything like this and simply buy a new phone, a good amount can be raised for the new phone by selling the old phone
 yani nayaa phone khareednaa he to pehle puraane ko thikaane lagaana hoga, lekin samajhadaari is baat main bhi he ki ham kaise apane puraane phone ko bechakar zyada se zyada rakam jutaayein taaki jeb se kam kharch karnaa pade

 lekin aise kai tips hai, jisase ham apane puraane gagetts ko bechakar uski sabase adhik keemat vasuul sakate hai
 1) First of all tie the knot that what is seen is sold
 yani aapkaa smartphone sahi condishan main dikhnaa chahie
 2) If the phone cover or case is old, scratch it, get a cheap but attractive phone case
 3) phone kaa original box, charger, data cabel saath ho to behatar deal paane main madad milti he
 4) Keep the phone clean and before selling, delete all your data, contacts etc
 from the phone
 5) behatar hoga agar phone ko factory riset kar den

 It is free and with the help of this, its product can be sold at a good price
 8) agar aap kisi retail outlet se phone exange kar rahe hai to behatar hoga, kai anya jagahon par bhi exange ophers kii jaanch kar len
 9) The festive season often attracts attractive exchange offers
 aap chahen to inkaa intjaar kar sakate hai
 10) Whenever a new and big brand phone is launched, still many new offers come, wait for them
 11) agar aapkaa smartphone varantee main he to yah sone par suhaaga he
 This helps in convincing the front-end customer and increases the chances of getting a better deal due to the warranty
 12) agar online deal kar rahe hai to email, massej or saare trek records ko sambhalakar rakhen
 13) Do not reset the call durations etc
 of your phone
 isse galat sanket jaataa he or graahak sankoch kar saktaa he ki phone kaa bahut istemaal hua he
 14) Uninstall all the apps and games from the phone except some important apps
 kam App hone par yahi samaj aata he ki phone kaa istemaal kam hua he
 15) If you have 'rooted' the phone in order to install an App, then 'unroot' it
